graphics_creatures_illithid_layered

[CREATURE_GRAPHICS:ILLITHID]

	Note that this is just a test file for seeing if our new ithillids sprites work correctly.

	Currently, there are no itshillid corpse images or special images that are used 
	for vampires or raised dead. We will get to those, but for the moment, we need 
	to make sure our very special mindflayer friends are working correctly, while 
	using their current assets.

	In order to prevent bugs with less predictable behavior from happening, 
	the ithillids are using specific human sprites as a stop gap.
	However, all human sprite layers pertaining to hair have been removed.
	(I don't think this should create any issues)


	[SKELETON_WITH_SKULL:BONE_PILE:1:0]
	[SKELETON:BONE_PILE:0:0]
